TITLE      Cross-Sections for inelastic scattering of neutrons on 2317300100007 
           Si-28 and comparison with the 25Mg(alpha,n)28Si        2317300100008 
           reaction.                                              2317300100009

FACILITY   (VDG,2ZZZGEL)  GELINA - Geel linear accelerator at     2317300100020 
            EC-JRC-IRMM. Frequency 800 Hz.                        2317300100021 
INC-SOURCE (PHOTO) Pulsed electron beam of 100 MeV on             2317300100022 
           depleted U target. Pulse duration 1 ns. Gamma flash is 2317300100023 
           generated via bremsstrahlung. Neutrons are produced    2317300100024 
           mainly by following gamma,n reaction.                  2317300100025 
           Collimated to 6.1 cm diameter at sample position.      2317300100026 
INC-SPECT   Neutron flux at sample position is of order           2317300100027 
           500 n/cm**2/s .                                        2317300100028 
SAMPLE     Natural sample of 1.326+-0.001 g/cm**2 .               2317300100029 
DETECTOR   (HPGE) GAINS detection system(Gamma Array for Inelastic2317300100030 
           Neutron Scattering) consists of eight HPGe detectors   2317300100031 
            (100% relative efficiency), placed at 110 and 150 deg 2317300100032 
           with respect to the neutron beam. Distance between the 2317300100033 
           center of the sample and the front side of each        2317300100034 
           detector is of the order of 15 cm. Read-out by four    2317300100035 
           DC440 Acquiris digitizers. Typical energy resolution of2317300100036 
           the large HPGe detectors read-out by the digitized     2317300100037 
           acquisition if of the order of 2.5 keV (FWHM) and the  2317300100038 
           time resolution is of the order of 8 ns.               2317300100039 
           Efficiency of the HPGe detectors is experimentally     2317300100040 
           determined using a calibrated Eu-152 source followed by2317300100041 
           the reproduction of the values using a detailed Monte  2317300100042 
           Carlo simulation of GAINS.                             2317300100043 
           (FISCH) Neutron beam is monitored using a 235U fission 2317300100044 
           chamber. Precise determination of the absolute         2317300100045 
           efficiency of the fission chamber is described in      2317300100046 
           REL-REF of A.Plompen+.                                 2317300100047 
REL-REF    (I,,A.Plompen+,J,KPS,59,(2),1581,2011) ND2010 Proc.    2317300100048 
           ND2010 paper #1373 of A.Plompen, page 177 in ND2010    2317300100049 
           Abstract book. Details of fission chamber.             2317300100050 
           (I,,D.Deleanu+,J,NIM/A,624,130,2010)                   2317300100051 
            Details of efficiency calibration procedure applied   2317300100052 
            to GAINS.                                             2317300100053 
           (R,,P.M.Endt,J,NP/A,633,1,1998)                        2317300100054 
            Level scheme used in analysis.                        2317300100055 
METHOD     (TOF,GSPEC) Sample was irradiated in cabin of Flight   2317300100056 
           path 3 situated at 200 m distance from neutron source  2317300100057 
           during 1000 hr.                                        2317300100058 
MONITOR    (92-U-235(N,F),,SIG)                                   2317300100059 
           From author: all our results are scaled to the         2317300100060 
           235U(n,F) cross section from ENDF/B-VII.1 .            2317300100061 
            Used for neutron flux monitoring.                     2317300100062 
MONIT-REF  (,,3,ENDF/B-VII.1,,2011)                               2317300100063 
ANALYSIS         The amplitude spectrum is used to identify the   2317300100064 
           transition while the time information determines the   2317300100065 
           energy of the incoming neutron that produced the       2317300100066 
           reaction. Monte Carlo simulations are used for the     2317300100067 
           determination of the HPGe detector efficiencies for the2317300100068 
           extended source and for the neutron multiple scattering2317300100069 
           correction. MCNP5 and GEANT4 codes were used.          2317300100070 
           For the calculation of level cross sections the        2317300100071 
           branching ratios and their uncertainties were taken    2317300100072 
           from ENSDF.                                            2317300100073 
CORRECTION  For the determination of the HPGe detector efficiency 2317300100074 
           for the extended source taking into account the        2317300100075 
           auto-absorption of the gammas in the sample and the    2317300100076 
           geometrical effect;                                    2317300100077 
           for the multiple scattering - of the order 5% at high  2317300100078 
           energies and almost negligible below 5 - 6 MeV.        2317300100079 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) Total uncertainty.                             2317300100080 
           From author: the most important sources of systematic  2317300100081 
           uncertainties come from:                               2317300100082 
           (ERR-1) the HPGe efficiency calibration (2%, which     2317300100083 
           includes a 0.7% contribution from the activity of the  2317300100084 
           calibration source), and                               2317300100085 
           (ERR-2) the Fission Chamber efficiency (2.1%).         2317300100086 
           (ERR-3) The sample thickness was known with very small 2317300100087 
           uncertainty (0.075%).                                  2317300100088 
           Uncertainty of monitor reaction cross section was also 2317300100089 
           considered.                                            2317300100090
